Did any one happen to remark\xe2\x80\x94as it went past\xe2\x80\x94three blue\r\nspots under each wing?\xe2\x80\x9d\r\n\r\nNobody had remarked them.\r\n\r\n\xe2\x80\x9cAh, well!\xe2\x80\x9d the Professor said with a sigh. \xe2\x80\x9cIt\xe2\x80\x99s a pity. Unless you\r\nremark that kind of thing _at the moment_, it\xe2\x80\x99s very apt to get\r\noverlooked! The _next_ Specimen, at any rate, will not fly away! It\r\nis\xe2\x80\x94in short, or perhaps, more correctly, at _length_\xe2\x80\x94an _Elephant_. You\r\nwill observe\xe2\x80\x94\xe2\x80\x94.\xe2\x80\x9d Here he beckoned to the Gardener to come up on the\r\nplatform, and with his help began putting together what looked like an\r\nenormous dog-kennel, with short tubes projecting out of it on both\r\nsides.\r\n\r\n\xe2\x80\x9cBut we\xe2\x80\x99ve seen _Elephants_ before,\xe2\x80\x9d the Emperor grumbled.\r\n\r\n\xe2\x80\x9cYes, but not through a _Megaloscope_!\xe2\x80\x9d the Professor eagerly replied.\r\n\xe2\x80\x9cYou know you can\xe2\x80\x99t see a _Flea_, properly, without a\r\n_magnifying_-glass\xe2\x80\x94what we call a _Microscope_. Well, just in the same\r\nway, you ca\xe2\x80\x99n\xe2\x80\x99t see an _Elephant_, properly, without a\r\n_minimifying_-glass. There\xe2\x80\x99s one in each of these little tubes. And\r\n_this_ is a _Megaloscope_! The Gardener will now bring in the next\r\nSpecimen. Please open _both_ curtains, down at the end there, and make\r\nway for the Elephant!\xe2\x80\x9d\r\n\r\nThere was a general rush to the sides of the Pavilion, and all eyes were\r\nturned to the open end, watching for the return of the Gardener, who had\r\ngone away singing \xe2\x80\x9c_He thought he saw an Elephant That practised on a\r\nFife!_\xe2\x80\x9d There was silence for a minute: and then his harsh voice was\r\nheard again in the distance. \xe2\x80\x9c_He looked again_\xe2\x80\x94come up, then! _He\r\nlooked again, and found it was_\xe2\x80\x94woa back! _and, found it was A letter\r\nfrom his_\xe2\x80\x94make way there! He\xe2\x80\x99s a-coming!\xe2\x80\x9d\r\n\r\n[Illustration: \xe2\x80\x98HE THOUGHT HE SAW AN ELEPHANT\xe2\x80\x99]\r\n\r\nAnd in marched, or waddled\xe2\x80\x94it is hard to say which is the right word\xe2\x80\x94an\r\nElephant, on its hind-legs, and playing on an enormous fife which it\r\nheld with its fore-feet.\r\n\r\nThe Professor hastily threw open a large door at the end of the\r\nMegaloscope, and the huge animal, at a signal from the Gardener, dropped\r\nthe fife, and obediently trotted into the machine, the door of which was\r\nat once shut by the Professor. \xe2\x80\x9cThe Specimen is now ready for\r\nobservation!\xe2\x80\x9d he proclaimed. \xe2\x80\x9cIt is exactly the size of the Common\r\nMouse\xe2\x80\x94_Mus Communis_!\xe2\x80\x9d\r\n\r\nThere was a general rush to the tubes, and the spectators watched with\r\ndelight the minikin creature, as it playfully coiled its trunk round the\r\nProfessor\xe2\x80\x99s extended finger, finally taking its stand upon the palm of\r\nhis hand, while he carefully lifted it out, and carried it off to\r\nexhibit to the Imperial party.\r\n\r\n\xe2\x80\x9cIsn\xe2\x80\x99t it a _darling_?\xe2\x80\x9d cried Bruno. \xe2\x80\x9cMay I stroke it, please? The door had swung open, and in\r\nanother moment the Monster had got out, and was trampling down the\r\nterrified, shrieking spectators.\r\n\r\nBut the Professor\xe2\x80\x99s presence of mind did not desert him. \xe2\x80\x9cUndraw those\r\ncurtains!\xe2\x80\x9d he shouted. It was done. The Monster gathered its legs\r\ntogether, and in one tremendous bound vanished into the sky.\r\n\r\n\xe2\x80\x9cWhere _is_ it?\xe2\x80\x9d said the Emperor, rubbing his eyes.\r\n\r\n\xe2\x80\x9cIn the next Province, I fancy,\xe2\x80\x9d the Professor replied. \xe2\x80\x9cThat jump would\r\ntake it at _least_ five miles! The next thing is to explain a Process or\r\ntwo. But I find there is hardly room enough to operate\xe2\x80\x94the smaller\r\nanimal is rather in my way\xe2\x80\x94\xe2\x80\x94\xe2\x80\x9d\r\n\r\n\xe2\x80\x9cWho does he mean?\xe2\x80\x9d Bruno whispered to Sylvie.\r\n\r\n\xe2\x80\x9cHe means _you_!\xe2\x80\x9d Sylvie whispered back. \xe2\x80\x9cHush!\xe2\x80\x9d\r\n\r\n\xe2\x80\x9cBe kind enough to move\xe2\x80\x94angularly\xe2\x80\x94to _this_ corner,\xe2\x80\x9d the Professor said,\r\naddressing himself to Bruno.\r\n\r\nBruno hastily moved his chair in the direction indicated. \xe2\x80\x9cDid I move\r\nangrily enough?\xe2\x80\x9d he inquired. But the Professor was once more absorbed\r\nin his Lecture, which he was reading from his note-book.\r\n\r\n\xe2\x80\x9cI will now explain the Process of\xe2\x80\x94the name is blotted, I\xe2\x80\x99m sorry to\r\nsay.
